Permanently disables the named factory by setting the corresponding\n   263→   * factory pointer to null. If the factory is registered under multiple\n   264→   * (deprecated) names, all the possible names are disabled.\n   265→   */\n   266→  static bool disableFactory(absl::string_view name) {\n   267→    const auto disable = [](absl::string_view name) -> bool {\n   268→      auto it = factories().find(name);\n   269→      if (it != factories().end()) {\n   270→        it->second = nullptr;\n   271→        return true;\n   272→      }\n   273→      return false;\n   274→    };\n   275→\n   276→    // First, find the canonical name for this factory.\n   277→    absl::string_view canonicalName = canonicalFactoryName(name);\n   278→\n   279→    // Next, disable the factory by all its deprecated names.\n   280→    for (const auto& [deprecated_name, mapped_canonical_name] : deprecatedFactoryNames()) {\n   281→      if (mapped_canonical_name == canonicalName) {\n   282→        disable(deprecated_name);\n   283→      }\n   284→    }\n   285→\n   286→    // Finally, disable the factory by its canonical name.\n   287→    return disable(canonicalName);\n   288→  }\n   289→\n   290→  /**\n   291→   * Gets a factory by name. If the name isn't found in the registry, returns nullptr.\n   292→   */\n   293→  static Base* getFactory(absl::string_view name) {\n   294→    auto it = factories().find(name);\n   295→    if (it == factories().end()) {\n   296→      return nullptr;\n   297→    }\n   298→\n   299→    return it->second;\n   300→  }\n   301→\n   302→  static Base* getFactoryByType(absl::string_view type) {\n   303→    auto it = factoriesByType().find(type);\n   304→    if (it == factoriesByType().end()) {\n   305→      return nullptr;\n   306→    }\n   307→    return it->second;\n   308→  }\n   309→\n   310→  /**\n   311→   * @return the canonical name of the factory. If the given name is a\n   312→   * deprecated factory name, the canonical name is returned instead.\n   313→   */\n   314→  static absl::string_view canonicalFactoryName(absl::string_view name) {\n   315→    const auto it = deprecatedFactoryNames().find(name);\n   316→    return (it == deprecatedFactoryNames().end()) ? name : it->second;\n   317→  }\n   318→\n   319→  /**\n   320→   * @return true factories().end());\n   325→    return it->second == nullptr;\n   326→  }\n   327→\n   328→  /**\n   329→   * @return vendor specific version of a factory.\n   330→   */\n   331→  static versionedFactories().end()) {\n   335→      return absl::nullopt;\n   336→    }\n   337→    return it->second;\n   338→  }\n   339→\n   340→  /**\n   341→   * @return set of config type names indexed by the factory name.\n   342→   */\n   343→  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, std::vector<std::string>> registeredTypes() {\n   344→    absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, std::vector<std::string>> mapping;\n   345→    for (const auto& [config_type, factory] : factoriesByType()) {\n   346→      mapping[factory->name()].push_back(config_type);\n   347→    }\n   348→ std::unique_ptr<absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>> buildFactoriesByType() {\n   356→    auto mapping = std::make_unique<absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>>();\n   357→\n   358→    for (const auto& [factory_name, factory] : factories()) {\n   359→      UNREFERENCED_PARAMETER(factory_name);\n   360→      if (factory == nullptr) {\n   361→        continue;\n   362→      }\n   363→\n   364→      for (const auto& config_type : factory->configTypes()) {\n   365→        ASSERT(!config_type.empty(), \"Extension config types can never be empty string\");\n   366→\n   367→        // Register config types in the mapping.\n   368→        auto it = mapping->find(config_type);\n   369→        if (it != mapping->end() && it->second != factory) {\n   370→          // Mark }\n   380→    }\n   381→\n   382→    return mapping;\n   383→  }\n   384→\n   385→  // Rebuild the factories-by-type map based on the current factories.\n   386→  static void  402→  replaceFactoryForTest(Base& factory,\n   403→                        std::initializer_list<absl::string_view> deprecated_names = {}) {\n   404→    using DeprecatedNamesVector =       ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Deprecated name '{}' (mapped to '{}')\", deprecated_name, factory.name());\n   442→        }\n   443→\n   444→        // Register the replacement factory with a deprecated by deprecated name failed\");\n   448→\n   449→        // Register the replacement factory's deprecated name.\n   450→        deprecatedFactoryNames().emplace(std::make_pair(deprecated_name, 457→      // Unregister the replacement factory by name.\n   458→      factories().erase(replacement->name());\n   459→\n   460→      ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Removed test factory '{}' (type '{}')\", replacement->name(),\n   461→                replacement->configTypes());\n   462→\n   463→      if (prev_by_name) {\n   464→        // Restore any factory displaced by name, but only register the 475→\n   476→        if (!mapped_canonical_name.empty()) {\n   477→          deprecatedFactoryNames().emplace(\n   478→              std::make_pair(prev_deprecated_name, mapped_canonical_name));\n   479→\n   480→          auto* deprecated_factory = getFactory(mapped_canonical_name);\n   481→          RELEASE_ASSERT(deprecated_factory != nullptr,\n   482→                         \"failed to ret.reserve(factories().size());\n\n    for (const auto& [factory_name, factory] : factories()) {\n      if (factory || include_disabled) {\n        ret.push_back(factory_name);\n      }\n    }\n\n    std::sort(ret.begin(), ret.end());\n\n    return ret;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gets the current map of factory implementations.\n   */\n  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>& factories() {\n    static auto* factories = new absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>;\n    return *factories;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gets the current map of vendor specific factory versions.\n   */\n  static envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion>;\n    MUTABLE_CONSTRUCT_ON_FIRST_USE(VersionedFactoryMap);\n  }\n\n  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, std::string>& deprecatedFactoryNames() {\n    static auto* deprecated_factory_names = new absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, std::string>;\n    return *deprecated_factory_names;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Lazily constructs a mapping from the configuration message type to a factory,\n   * including the deprecated configuration message types.\n   * Must be invoked after factory registration is completed.\n   */\n  static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>& factoriesByType() {\n    static absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>* factories_by_type =\n        buildFactoriesByType().release();\n\n    return *factories_by_type;\n  }\n\n  static bool& allowDuplicates() {\n    static bool* allow_duplicates = new bool(false);\n    return *allow_duplicates;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * instead_value are used when passed name was deprecated.\n   */\n  static void registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name,\n                              absl::string_view instead_value = \"\") {\n    auto result = factories().emplace(std::make_pair(name, &factory));\n    if (!result.second && !allowDuplicates()) {\n      ExceptionUtil::throwEnvoyException(\n          fmt::format(\"Double registration for name: '{}'\", factory.name()));\n    }\n\n are versioned\n   * independently of Envoy.\n   */\n  static void registerFactory(Base& factory, absl::string_view name,\n                              const envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion& corresponding\n   * factory pointer to null. If the factory is registered under multiple\n   * (deprecated) names, all the possible names are disabled.\n   */\n  static bool disableFactory(absl::string_view name) {\n    const auto disable = [](absl::string_view name) -> bool {\n      auto it = factories().find(name);\n      if (it != factories().end()) {\n        it->second = nullptr;\n        return true;\n      }\n      return false;\n    };\n\n    // First, find the canonical name for this factory.\n    absl::string_view canonicalName = canonicalFactoryName(name);\n\n    // Next, disable the factory by all its deprecated names.\n    for (const auto& [deprecated_name, mapped_canonical_name] : deprecatedFactoryNames()) {\n      if (mapped_canonical_name == canonicalName) {\n        disable(deprecated_name);\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Finally, disable the factory by its canonical name.\n    return disable(canonicalName);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gets a factory by name. If the name isn't found in the registry, returns nullptr.\n   */\n  static Base* getFactory(absl::string_view name) {\n    auto it = factories().find(name);\n    if (it == factories().end()) {\n      return nullptr;\n    }\n\n    return it->second;\n  }\n\n  static Base* getFactoryByType(absl::string_view type) {\n    auto it = factoriesByType().find(type);\n    if (it == factoriesByType().end()) {\n      return nullptr;\n    }\n    return it->second;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * @return the canonical name of the factory. deprecatedFactoryNames().find(name);\n    return (it == deprecatedFactoryNames().end()) ? name : it->second;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * @return true if the named factory was disabled.\n   */\n  static bool isFactoryDisabled(absl::string_view name) {\n    auto it = factories().find(name);\n    ASSERT(it != factories().end());\n    return it->second == nullptr;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * @return vendor specific version of a factory.\n   */\n  static absl::optional<envoy::config::core::v3::BuildVersion>\n  getFactoryVersion(absl::string_view name) {\n    auto it = versionedFactories().find(name);\n    if (it factoriesByType()) {\n      mapping[factory->name()].push_back(config_type);\n    }\n    return mapping;\n  }\n\nprivate:\n  // Allow factory injection only in tests.\n  friend class InjectFactory<Base>;\n\n  static std::unique_ptr<absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>> buildFactoriesByType() {\n    auto mapping = std::make_unique<absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, Base*>>();\n\n    for (const auto& [factory_name, factory] : factories()) {\n      UNREFERENCED_PARAMETER(factory_name);\n      if (factory == nullptr) {\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      for (const auto& config_type : factory->configTypes()) {\n        ASSERT(!config_type.empty(), \"Extension config types can never be empty string\");\n\n        // Register config types in the mapping.\n        auto it = mapping->find(config_type);\n        if (it != mapping->end() && it->second != factory) {\n          // Mark double-registered types with a nullptr for tests only.\n          // See issue https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/issues/9643.\n          RELEASE_ASSERT(false, fmt::format(\"Double registration for type: '{}' by '{}' and '{}'\",\n                                            config_type, factory->name(),\n                                            it->second ? it->second->name() : \"\"));\n          it->second = nullptr;\n        } else {\n          mapping->emplace(std::make_pair(config_type, factory));\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    return mapping;\n  }\n\n  // Rebuild the factories-by-type map based on the current factories.\n  static void rebuildFactoriesByTypeForTest() {\n    auto& mapping = factoriesByType();\n    auto updated_mapping = buildFactoriesByType();\n\n    // Copy the updated mapping over the old one.\n    mapping = *updated_mapping;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Replaces a factory by name.                        std::initializer_list<absl::string_view> deprecated_names = {}) {\n    using DeprecatedNamesVector = std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::string>>;\n\n    // If an existing prev_by_name->name(), prev_by_name->configTypes(), factory.name(), factory.configTypes());\n    } else {\n      ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Factory '{}' (type '{}') registered for tests\", factory.name(),\n                factory.configTypes());\n    }\n\n    factories().emplace(factory.name(), &factory);\n    RELEASE_ASSERT(getFactory(factory.name()) == &factory,\n                   \"test factory by-name deprecatedFactoryNames().emplace(std::make_pair(deprecated_name, factory.name()));\n      }\n    }\n\n    rebuildFactoriesByTypeForTest();\n\n    return [replacement = &factory, prev_by_name, prev_deprecated_names]() {\n      // Unregister the replacement factory by name.\n      factories().erase(replacement->name());\n\n      ENVOY_LOG(info, \"Removed test factory '{}' (type '{}')\", MessageUtil::unpackToOrThrow(typed_config, typed_struct);\n      // Not handling nested structs or typed structs in typed structs\n      return lookup by factory name\\n   - Returns pointer to registered factory instance (or nullptr if not found)\\n\\n5. **Factory Invocation**: The returned factory pointer is called with the configuration to create the actual filter instance\\n\\n## Key Files Implementing the Pattern\\n\\n- **envoy/registry/registry.h**: Core Registry<Base> template and RegisterFactory<T, Base> class, REGISTER_FACTORY instance declaration\\n\\n2. **Static Object Construction**: When the translation unit is linked, the RegisterFactory<ChecksumFilterFactory, NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory> instance is constructed\\n\\n3. **Registration**: RegisterFactory constructor:\\n   - Calls FactoryRegistry<NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory>::registerFactory(instance_, instance_.name())\\n   - Stores reference to factory instance in factories() static hash map\\n   - Calls FactoryCategoryRegistry::registerCategory() to register the category\\n   - Uses ASSERT to verify factory name is not empty\\n\\n4. lookup by factory name\\n   - Returns pointer to registered factory instance (or nullptr if not found)\\n\\n5. **Factory Invocation**: The returned factory pointer is called with the configuration to create the actual filter instance\\n\\n## Key Files Implementing the Pattern\\n\\n- **envoy/registry/registry.h**: Core Registry<Base> template and RegisterFactory<T, Base> class, REGISTER_FACTORY category is managed by a FactoryRegistryProxy instance\\n- Prevents double registration of categories\\n- Exposes factory names per category through registeredNames() method\\n\\n## Factory Inheritance Hierarchy\\n\\n**Base Classes** (envoy/config/typed_config.h):\\n- UntypedFactory: Base class with name(), category(), and configTypes() methods\\n- TypedFactory: Adds
